the McDonald&#8217;s 401(k) Plan (the &#8220;Plan&#8221;), participants in the Plan&#160;will be&#160;unable,&#160;for a period of time, to&#160;transfer&#160;or diversify investments in their accounts,&#160;or&#160;obtain a loan,&#160;withdrawal or distribution from the Plan. The&#160;temporary&#160;blackout period&#160;for participants under the Plan&#160;begins&#160;at&#160;4:00 p.m.&#160;Eastern&#160;Time,&#160;January 13, 2017,&#160;and is expected to end on January 19, 2017. &#160;The blackout period applies&#160;to all Plan assets, including Company shares held by the Plan.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">On December 28, 2016, the Company sent an appropriate notice&#160;(the &#8220;Notice&#8221;)&#160;to its directors and executive officers&#160;informing them of the blackout period and the restrictions on trading in&#160;McDonald's Corporation&#160;common stock&#160;that apply to them during the blackout period, pursuant to Section&#160;306(a)&#160;of the Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002 and Rule&#160;104 of Regulation BTR&#160;under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934.&#160; A copy of the Notice is attached as Exhibit&#160;99 to this Form&#160;8-K and is incorporated by reference.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Company stockholders or other interested persons may obtain information about the actual dates of the blackout period, without charge, by contacting the Company&#8217;s Corporate Legal Department by phone at 630-623-3000 or by mail c/o McDonald&#8217;s Corporation, 2915 Jorie Blvd, Oak Brook, IL 60523 during this blackout period and for a period of two years after its ending date.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Item&#160;9.01. <DESCRIPTION>NOTICE
<TEXT>
<!DOCTYPE html PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd">
<html>
	<head>
		<!-- Document created using Wdesk 1 -->

	<body style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">
<div><a name="sF6CB7D6CCC855038BB91AE79566A5EE2"></a></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><div><br></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Important Notice to Directors and Executive Officers</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Of McDonald&#8217;s Corporation (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Concerning Additional Legal Restrictions on Their Personal Trading in Company Stock </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">December 28, 2016</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Federal securities laws require the Company to provide this notice to its Directors and Executive Officers.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">In connection with a change to the investment alternatives available under the Company&#8217;s 401(k) Plan (the &#8220;401(k) Plan&#8221;), there will be a blackout period for 401(k) Plan participants scheduled to begin on January&#160;13, 2017 at 4:00 p.m. Eastern Time and expected to end on January&#160;19, 2017 (&#8220;Plan Blackout Period&#8221;).  During the Plan Blackout Period, 401(k) Plan participants will not be permitted to&#160;transfer&#160;or diversify investments in their accounts and will not be permitted to request a loan, distribution, or withdrawal.  The blackout is required in order to implement the changes to the investment alternatives as well as for administrative and technology reasons.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:16px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Under federal law, during the Plan Blackout Period, Directors and Executive Officers will be prohibited from directly or indirectly purchasing, selling, or otherwise acquiring, disposing or transferring shares of McDonald's Corporation common stock or derivative securities, acquired in connection with their service as a Director or Executive Officer of McDonald&#8217;s (&#8220;Compensatory Shares&#8221;).  These restrictions include indirect transactions by family members, partnerships, corporations, trusts or others involving Compensatory Shares where the Director or Executive Officer has a pecuniary interest.  There are limited exceptions to these restrictions (e.g., sales pursuant to court orders or as required by law).  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Please note that during the Plan Blackout Period, the Company&#8217;s trading window will be closed.  As a result, the restrictions referred to above are duplicative of trading prohibitions that already apply to Directors and Executive Officers during this period.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:16px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Please contact Denise Horne (by telephone at 630-623-3000 or by mail c/o McDonald&#8217;s Corporation, 2915 Jorie Blvd, Oak Brook, IL 60523) for additional information or if you have any questions regarding the Plan Blackout Period.</font></div><div><br></div><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div>	</body>
